#### æ—¥å¿—å†…å®¹è¦æ±‚

- **é”™è¯¯ç æ ¼å¼**ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ç»Ÿä¸€çš„é”™è¯¯ç æ ¼å¼ï¼ˆå¦‚ `ERR_USER_NOT_FOUND`ã€`ERR_INVALID_INPUT`ï¼‰

```javascript
    USER_NOT_FOUND: 'ERR_USER_NOT_FOUND',
    INVALID_INPUT: 'ERR_INVALID_INPUT',
    DATABASE_ERROR: 'ERR_DATABASE_ERROR',
    NETWORK_ERROR: 'ERR_NETWORK_ERROR'
};

function getUserById(userId) {
    try {
        const user = fetchUser(userId);
        if (!user) {
            throw new AppError(ErrorCodes.USER_NOT_FOUND, 'ç”¨æˆ·ä¸å­˜åœ¨');
        }
        return user;
    } catch (error) {
        if (error.code === ErrorCodes.USER_NOT_FOUND) {
            return {
                success: false,
                code: ErrorCodes.USER_NOT_FOUND,
                message: 'æœªæ‰¾åˆ°ç”¨æˆ·ä¿¡æ¯'
            };
        }
        throw error;
    }
}
```

#### é”™è¯¯ä¿¡æ¯å›½é™…åŒ–

å¦‚æœåº”ç”¨æ”¯æŒå¤šè¯­è¨€ï¼Œé”™è¯¯ä¿¡æ¯åº”æ”¯æŒå›½é™…åŒ–ï¼š

- **å ä½ç¬¦æ”¯æŒ**ï¼šæ”¯æŒåœ¨é”™è¯¯ä¿¡æ¯ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨å ä½ç¬¦ï¼ŒåŠ¨æ€å¡«å……å˜é‡

```javascript
        INVALID_INPUT: 'è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®æ— æ•ˆ'
```

**æ¨¡å¼3ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ Result ç±»å‹**

```typescript
// âœ… å¥½çš„åšæ³•ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ Result ç±»å‹ï¼ˆTypeScriptï¼‰
type Result<T, E> = 
    | { success: true; data: T }
    | { success: false; error: E };

function getUserById(userId: string): Result<User, string> {
    try {
        const user = fetchUser(userId);
        if (!user) {
            return { success: false, error: 'USER_NOT_FOUND' };
        }
        return { success: true, data: user };
    } catch (error) {
        return { success: false, error: 'DATABASE_ERROR' };
    }
}
```

- **ç»Ÿä¸€é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†æœºåˆ¶**ï¼šåœ¨ä»£ç ä¸­å®ç°ç»Ÿä¸€çš„é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†æœºåˆ¶ï¼Œç¡®ä¿æ‰€æœ‰å¯èƒ½çš„é”™è¯¯æƒ…å†µéƒ½è¢«æ•è·å’Œå¤„ç†

  - âŒ **é—®é¢˜ä¿®å¤**ï¼šä¿®å¤å·²å­˜åœ¨çš„é—®é¢˜æ—¶ï¼Œåº”å…ˆéµå¾ª `problem-location.md` å®šä½é—®é¢˜ï¼Œå†æ ¹æ®å®šä½ç»“æœæ·»åŠ å¿…è¦çš„é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†

#### å¼‚å¸¸æ•è·è§„èŒƒ

**âœ… å¥½çš„åšæ³•ï¼šæ•è·å…·ä½“å¼‚å¸¸ç±»å‹**

```javascript
    return processData(data);

    if (error instanceof SyntaxError) {
        // å¤„ç† JSON è§£æé”™è¯¯
        logger.error('JSON è§£æå¤±è´¥', { error, jsonString });
        throw new ValidationError('æ— æ•ˆçš„ JSON æ ¼å¼');
    } else if (error instanceof TypeError) {
        // å¤„ç†ç±»å‹é”™è¯¯
        logger.error('ç±»å‹é”™è¯¯', { error });
        throw new ValidationError('æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ä¸æ­£ç¡®');
    } else {
        // å¤„ç†å…¶ä»–æœªçŸ¥é”™è¯¯
        logger.error('æœªçŸ¥é”™è¯¯', { error });
        throw error;
```

```python

    return process_data(data)
```

#### é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†æ¨¡å¼

**æ¨¡å¼1ï¼šç«‹å³å¤„ç†å¹¶è¿”å›**

**æ¨¡å¼2ï¼šå¤„ç†å¹¶æŠ›å‡ºæ–°çš„é”™è¯¯**

```javascript

function validateUserData(userData) {
    try {
        validateEmail(userData.email);
        validatePhone(userData.phone);
        return true;
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error('ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®éªŒè¯å¤±è´¥', { userData, error });
        throw new ValidationError('ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®æ— æ•ˆ', { cause: error });
    }
}
```

**æ¨¡å¼3ï¼šé”™è¯¯æ¢å¤**

```javascript
// âœ… å¥½çš„åšæ³•ï¼šå®ç°é”™è¯¯æ¢å¤æœºåˆ¶
async function fetchUserData(userId) {
    try {
        return await fetchFromPrimaryDatabase(userId);
    } catch (error) {
        logger.warn('ä¸»æ•°æ®åº“æŸ¥è¯¢å¤±è´¥ï¼Œå°è¯•å¤‡ç”¨æ•°æ®åº“', { userId, error });
        try {
            return await fetchFromBackupDatabase(userId);
        } catch (backupError) {
            logger.error('å¤‡ç”¨æ•°æ®åº“æŸ¥è¯¢ä¹Ÿå¤±è´¥', { userId, error: backupError });
            throw new DatabaseError('æ— æ³•è·å–ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®', { cause: backupError });
        }

}
```

#### é”™è¯¯è¾¹ç•Œå¤„ç†

- **è¾¹ç•Œæ£€æŸ¥**ï¼šåœ¨å‡½æ•°å…¥å£å¤„è¿›è¡Œå‚æ•°éªŒè¯ï¼Œé¿å…æ— æ•ˆè¾“å…¥å¯¼è‡´é”™è¯¯
- **èµ„æºæ¸…ç†**ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ `finally` å—ç¡®ä¿èµ„æºè¢«æ­£ç¡®æ¸…ç†
- **é”™è¯¯ä¼ æ’­**ï¼šåˆç†å†³å®šæ˜¯å¦å‘ä¸Šä¼ æ’­é”™è¯¯ï¼Œè¿˜æ˜¯å°±åœ°å¤„ç†

**ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š

```javascript
// âœ… å¥½çš„åšæ³•ï¼šè¾¹ç•Œæ£€æŸ¥å’Œèµ„æºæ¸…ç†
async function processFile(filePath) {
    // è¾¹ç•Œæ£€æŸ¥
    if (!filePath || typeof filePath !== 'string') {
        throw new ValidationError('æ–‡ä»¶è·¯å¾„æ— æ•ˆ');
    }

    let fileHandle = null;
    try {
        fileHandle = await openFile(filePath);
        const content = await readFile(fileHandle);
        return processContent(content);
    } catch (error) {
        logger.error('æ–‡ä»¶å¤„ç†å¤±è´¥', { filePath, error });
        throw new ProcessingError('æ— æ³•å¤„ç†æ–‡ä»¶', { cause: error });
    } finally {
        // ç¡®ä¿èµ„æºè¢«æ¸…ç†
        if (fileHandle) {
            await closeFile(fileHandle);
        }
    }
}
```

```javascript
// âŒ ä¸å¥½çš„åšæ³•ï¼šåµŒå¥—é€»è¾‘
function processUsers(users) {
  return users.map(user => {
    if (user.isActive) {
      return user.data.map(item => {
        if (item.valid) {
          return processItem(item);
        }
      });
    }
  });
}

// âœ… å¥½çš„åšæ³•ï¼šæå–å‡½æ•°
function processUsers(users) {
  return users
    .filter(isActiveUser)
    .flatMap(getUserData)
    .filter(isValidItem)
    .map(processItem);
}

function isActiveUser(user) {
  return user.isActive;
}

function getUserData(user) {
  return user.data;
}

function isValidItem(item) {
  return item.valid;
}
```

```javascript
    if (users[i].isActive) {
      result.push(users[i].name);
    }
  }
  return result;
```

#### âŒ ç¦æ­¢æ·»åŠ ä¸å¿…è¦çš„ try-catch

##### 1.2 è·å–æ—¶é—´çš„æ–¹æ³•

**JavaScript è·å–å½“å‰æ—¥æœŸ**ï¼š

```javascript
  month: '2-digit',
  day: '2-digit'

// è·å– YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS æ ¼å¼

  month: '2-digit',
  day: '2-digit',
  hour: '2-digit',
  minute: '2-digit',
  second: '2-digit',
  hour12: false
```

**TypeScript è·å–å½“å‰æ—¶é—´**ï¼š
```typescript

  const now = new Date();
  const year = now.getFullYear();
  const month = String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const day = String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
};
```

     - âŒ æ ¼å¼å ä½ç¬¦ï¼ˆå¦‚ `YYYY-MM-DD`ï¼‰

     - âŒ ä¸å…ˆè·å–å°±å¡«å†™çš„ä»»ä½•æ—¥æœŸ

**å¼ºåˆ¶æ£€æŸ¥æ¸…å•**ï¼ˆæ¯æ¬¡å†™å…¥æ–‡ä»¶å‰å¿…æŸ¥ï¼‰ï¼š

- [ ] **å·²è¯†åˆ«æ–‡æ¡£ä¸­çš„æ—¶é—´å­—æ®µ**
